RESPONSE:
To decide on the best action for building the initial settlement, we need to consider several factors:
1. **Resource Diversity:** Placing a settlement where it can generate a variety of resources.
2. **Probability of Resource Production:** Tiles with higher dice numbers (5-9) have a higher probability of producing resources.
3. **Access to Ports:** Placing a settlement near ports can facilitate better trading rates.
4. **Future Expansion:** Considering nodes that allow for strategic expansion in future turns.

Let's analyze a few promising nodes:

- **Node 3:** Access to 🌾6, 🐑4, 🌲2. The 🌲2 tile has a low probability, but access to 🌾6 and 🐑4 is good. It's also near the 🧱BRICK port (nodes 28, 29).
- **Node 10:** Access to 🌾5, 🐑8, ⛏️11. High probability tiles and diverse resources. Near the 🐑SHEEP port (nodes 32, 33).
- **Node 11:** Access to 🌾6, 🐑4, 🌾5. Good wheat production but lacks diversity. Near the 🐑SHEEP port (nodes 32, 33).
- **Node 13:** Access to 🌾9, 🐑4, 🌲9. High probability tiles and diverse resources. Near the ⛏️ORE port (nodes 35, 36).
- **Node 20:** Access to 🌲2, 🌾12, 🌲11. Good wood production but 🌲2 has a low probability. Near the 🌲WOOD port (nodes 45, 47).

Considering resource diversity, probability, and access to ports, **Node 13** stands out as a strong candidate. It provides access to high probability tiles for 🌾WHEAT, 🐑SHEEP, and 🌲WOOD, and it is near the ⛏️ORE port, which can be beneficial for trading later in the game.

<plan>Build the initial settlement at Node 13 to secure diverse and high probability resource production. Plan to expand towards the ⛏️ORE port and consider future settlements that can benefit from the 🌲WOOD port.</plan>

     - Settlement at node 35: Produces ⛏️4.

     - Settlement at node 8: Produces 🌲8, 🐑8, ⛏️11.
     - Settlement at node 15: Produces 🌾9, 🧱10, 🐑5.

   - We need to identify the best hex to place the robber to maximize disruption to RED while minimizing disruption to BLUE.
   - **RED's Key Resources:**
     - 🌲8 (1, -1, 0) is a crucial resource for RED, as it produces 3 resources for their settlement at node 8.
     - 🧱10 (-1, 1, 0) is another important resource for RED, as it produces 1 resource for their settlement at node 15.
     - ⛏️11 (1, -2, 1) is important for RED's settlement at node 8.

   - **[1] Move robber to (1, -1, 0) and steal from RED:**
     - This action blocks the 🌲8 resource for RED, significantly impacting their production.
     - Steals a resource from RED.

     - This action blocks the 🧱10 resource for RED, impacting their production.

     - This action blocks the ⛏️11 resource for RED, impacting their production.

   - Stealing a resource from RED will also benefit BLUE by reducing RED's ability to build and expand.

### Conclusion:

   - BLUE produces 🌾WHEAT, ⛏️ORE, and has access to the ⛏️ORE port.
   - RED has 4 settlements and is ahead in terms of road building and resource production diversity.

   - [0] Play Knight card - Move the robber and steal a resource.
   - [1] Roll the dice.

4. **Strategic Considerations**:
   - **Playing the Knight Card**:
     - Moving the robber can block RED's resource production.
     - Stealing a resource from RED can disrupt their plans.
     - This action can slow down RED's progress and potentially gain a resource for BLUE.
   - **Rolling the Dice**:
     - Rolling the dice can gain resources if the dice roll favors the tiles BLUE has settlements on.
     - However, RED also has a chance to gain resources, potentially accelerating their progress.

5. **Next 2-3 Turns**:
   - Playing the Knight card now can give BLUE an immediate advantage by blocking RED's resource production and stealing a resource.
   - After playing the Knight card, BLUE can then focus on building roads towards the ⛏️ORE port and securing it.
   - Once the port is secured, BLUE can trade resources more effectively and work towards upgrading settlements to cities.

6. **Final Decision**:
   - Playing the Knight card is the best immediate action to disrupt RED's progress and potentially gain a resource.

   - This action aligns with your current plan and gets you closer to your goal of reaching the 3:1 port.

1. **Current Plan**:
   - Continue to build a road towards the 3:1 port, then focus on acquiring resources to buy development cards and upgrade settlements to cities. Prioritize collecting 🧱 BRICK and 🌲 WOOD.

2. **Game State**:
   - We are at the initial settlement building phase.
   - No resources or development cards are currently held.
   - The robber is at (2, 0, -2), blocking the ⛏️ ORE tile with a dice number of 6.

3. **Resource and Node Analysis**:
   - We need to maximize resource gain, especially 🧱 BRICK and 🌲 WOOD.
   - Nodes connected to high-probability resource tiles (dice numbers 6 and 8) are preferable.
   - Considering the plan to build towards the 3:1 port, nodes 35, 36, 38, and 39 are key.

4. **Settlement Placement Options**:
   - **Node 35**: Connected to 🌲 WOOD (8) and near the 3:1 port.
   - **Node 36**: Connected to 🌲 WOOD (8) and near the 3:1 port.
   - **Node 38**: Connected to 🧱 BRICK (10) and near the 3:1 port.
   - **Node 39**: Connected to 🧱 BRICK (10) and near the 3:1 port.

5. **Strategic Considerations**:
   - Placing a settlement at node 35 or 36 will give access to 🌲 WOOD (8), which is crucial for our plan.
   - Placing a settlement at node 38 or 39 will give access to 🧱 BRICK (10), also crucial for our plan.
   - Both options are near the 3:1 port, facilitating future trades.

6. **Decision**:
   - Given the importance of 🌲 WOOD for initial road building and the slightly higher probability of the dice number 8 compared to 10, placing a settlement at node 35 or 36 is strategically better.
   - Node 35 is chosen arbitrarily between the two equally good options.

Therefore, the chosen action is:

   - Option [5]: Building at edge (13, 34) is less strategic as it doesn't move you towards the port or block RED significantly.

   - The immediate benefit of building a road towards a port is significant for long-term resource management.
